#########################################
#  TRAIT NOTIFICATION SCRIPTED EFFECTS  #
#########################################


#### [1] Amateurish Plotter: amateurish_plotter ####
emf_notify_add_amateurish_plotter_effect = {
	#hidden_tooltip = {
	#	if = {
	#		limit = { trait = amateurish_plotter }
	#		log = "WARNING: emf_notify_add_amateurish_plotter_effect: [This.GetBestName] ([This.GetID]) already has the trait to be added!"
	#	}
	#}
	if = {
		limit = { NOT = { trait = amateurish_plotter } }
		add_trait = amateurish_plotter
		hidden_tooltip = {
			if = {
				limit = { ai = no }
				save_event_target_as = emf_notify_char
				character_event = { id = emf_notify.1 }
				clear_event_target = emf_notify_char
			}
			ROOT = {
				if = {
					limit = {
						ai = no
						NOT = { character = PREV }
					}
					save_event_target_as = emf_notify_char
					PREV = { character_event = { id = emf_notify.1 } }
					clear_event_target = emf_notify_char
				}
			}
			event_target:emf_notify_receiver = {
				if = {
					limit = {
						ai = no
						NOT = { character = PREV }
						NOT = { character = ROOT }
					}
					save_event_target_as = emf_notify_char
					PREV = { character_event = { id = emf_notify.1 } }
					clear_event_target = emf_notify_char
				}
			}
		}
	}
}
emf_notify_remove_amateurish_plotter_effect = {
	#hidden_tooltip = {
	#	if = {
	#		limit = { NOT = { trait = amateurish_plotter } }
	#		log = "WARNING: emf_notify_remove_amateurish_plotter_effect: [This.GetBestName] ([This.GetID]) doesn't have the trait to be removed!"
	#	}
	#}
	if = {
		limit = { trait = amateurish_plotter }
		remove_trait = amateurish_plotter
		hidden_tooltip = {
			if = {
				limit = { ai = no }
				save_event_target_as = emf_notify_char
				character_event = { id = emf_notify.1001 }
				clear_event_target = emf_notify_char
			}
			ROOT = {
				if = {
					limit = {
						ai = no
						NOT = { character = PREV }
					}
					save_event_target_as = emf_notify_char
					PREV = { character_event = { id = emf_notify.1001 } }
					clear_event_target = emf_notify_char
				}
			}
			event_target:emf_notify_receiver = {
				if = {
					limit = {
						ai = no
						NOT = { character = PREV }
						NOT = { character = ROOT }
					}
					save_event_target_as = emf_notify_char
					PREV = { character_event = { id = emf_notify.1001 } }
					clear_event_target = emf_notify_char
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

	#hidden_tooltip = {
	#	if = {
	#		limit = { trait = cruel }
	#		log = "WARNING: emf_notify_add_cruel_effect: [This.GetBestName] ([This.GetID]) already has the trait to be added!"
	#	}
	#}
	if = {
		limit = { NOT = { trait = cruel } }
		add_trait = cruel
		hidden_tooltip = {
			if = {
				limit = { ai = no }
				save_event_target_as = emf_notify_char
				character_event = { id = emf_notify.101 }
				clear_event_target = emf_notify_char
			}
			ROOT = {
				if = {
					limit = {
						ai = no
						NOT = { character = PREV }
					}
					save_event_target_as = emf_notify_char
					PREV = { character_event = { id = emf_notify.101 } }
					clear_event_target = emf_notify_char
				}
			}
			event_target:emf_notify_receiver = {
				if = {
					limit = {
						ai = no
						NOT = { character = PREV }
						NOT = { character = ROOT }
					}
					save_event_target_as = emf_notify_char
					PREV = { character_event = { id = emf_notify.101 } }
					clear_event_target = emf_notify_char
				}
			}
		}
	}
}
emf_notify_remove_cruel_effect = {
	#hidden_tooltip = {
	#	if = {

	#		log = "WARNING: emf_notify_remove_cruel_effect: [This.GetBestName] ([This.GetID]) doesn't have the trait to be removed!"
	#	}
	#}
	if = {
		limit = { trait = cruel }
		remove_trait = cruel
		hidden_tooltip = {
			if = {
				limit = { ai = no }
				save_event_target_as = emf_notify_char

	#		limit = { NOT = { trait = skilled_diplomat } }
	#		log = "WARNING: emf_notify_remove_skilled_diplomat_effect: [This.GetBestName] ([This.GetID]) doesn't have the trait to be removed!"
	#	}
	#}

		limit = { trait = skilled_diplomat }
		remove_trait = skilled_diplomat
		hidden_tooltip = {
			if = {
				limit = { ai = no }
				save_event_target_as = emf_notify_char
				character_event = { id = emf_notify.1242 }
				clear_event_target = emf_notify_char
			}
			ROOT = {
				if = {
					limit = {
						ai = no
						NOT = { character = PREV }
					}
					save_event_target_as = emf_notify_char
					PREV = { character_event = { id = emf_notify.1242 } }
					clear_event_target = emf_notify_char
				}
			}
			event_target:emf_notify_receiver = {
				if = {
					limit = {
						ai = no
						NOT = { character = PREV }
						NOT = { character = ROOT }
					}
					save_event_target_as = emf_notify_char
					PREV = { character_event = { id = emf_notify.1242 } }
					clear_event_target = emf_notify_char

emf_notify_add_reincarnated_effect = {
	#hidden_tooltip = {
	#	if = {
	#		limit = { trait = reincarnated }
	#		log = "WARNING: emf_notify_add_reincarnated_effect: [This.GetBestName] ([This.GetID]) already has the trait to be added!"
	#	}
	#}
	if = {
		limit = { NOT = { trait = reincarnated } }
		add_trait = reincarnated
		hidden_tooltip = {
			if = {
				limit = { ai = no }
				save_event_target_as = emf_notify_char
				character_event = { id = emf_notify.308 }
				clear_event_target = emf_notify_char
			}
			ROOT = {
				if = {
					limit = {
						ai = no
						NOT = { character = PREV }
					}
					save_event_target_as = emf_notify_char
					PREV = { character_event = { id = emf_notify.308 } }
					clear_event_target = emf_notify_char
				}
			}
			event_target:emf_notify_receiver = {
				if = {
					limit = {
						ai = no
						NOT = { character = PREV }
						NOT = { character = ROOT }
					}
					save_event_target_as = emf_notify_char
					PREV = { character_event = { id = emf_notify.308 } }
					clear_event_target = emf_notify_char
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

		limit = { trait = lovers_pox }
		remove_trait = lovers_pox
		hidden_tooltip = {
			if = {
				limit = { ai = no }
				save_event_target_as = emf_notify_char
				character_event = { id = emf_notify.1333 }
				clear_event_target = emf_notify_char
			}
			ROOT = {
				if = {
					limit = {
						ai = no
						NOT = { character = PREV }
					}
					save_event_target_as = emf_notify_char
					PREV = { character_event = { id = emf_notify.1333 } }
					clear_event_target = emf_notify_char
				}
			}
			event_target:emf_notify_receiver = {
				if = {
					limit = {
						ai = no
						NOT = { character = PREV }
						NOT = { character = ROOT }
					}
					save_event_target_as = emf_notify_char
					PREV = { character_event = { id = emf_notify.1333 } }
					clear_event_target = emf_notify_char
				}
			}
		}
	}
}
